2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSwarm focuses on making agent \u003cstrong\u003ecoordination\u003c/strong\u003e and \u003cstrong\u003eexecution\u003c/strong\u003e lightweight, highly controllable, and easily testable.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIt accomplishes this through two primitive abstractions: \u003ccode\u003eAgent\u003c/code\u003es and \u003cstrong\u003ehandoffs\u003c/strong\u003e. An \u003ccode\u003eAgent\u003c/code\u003e encompasses \u003ccode\u003einstructions\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003etools\u003c/code\u003e, and can at any point choose to hand off a conversation to another \u003ccode\u003eAgent\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThese primitives are powerful enough to express rich dynamics between tools and networks of agents, allowing you to build scalable, real-world solutions while avoiding a steep learning curve.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-alert markdown-alert-note\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cp class=\"markdown-alert-title\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-info mr-2\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003eNote\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSwarm Agents are not related to Assistants in the Assistants API. They are named similarly for convenience, but are otherwise completely unrelated. Swarm is entirely powered by the Chat Completions API and is hence stateless between calls.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhy Swarm\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-why-swarm\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Why Swarm\" href=\"#why-swarm\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSwarm explores patterns that are lightweight, scalable, and highly customizable by design. Approaches similar to Swarm are best suited for situations dealing with a large number of independent capabilities and instructions that are difficult to encode into a single prompt.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe Assistants API is a great option for developers looking for fully-hosted threads and built in memory management and retrieval. However, Swarm is an educational resource for developers curious to learn about multi-agent orchestration. Swarm runs (almost) entirely on the client and, much like the Chat Completions API, does not store state between calls.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch1 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eExamples\u003c/h1\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-examples\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Examples\" href=\"#examples\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eCheck out \u003ccode\u003e/examples\u003c/code\u003e for inspiration! instantiates an \u003ccode\u003eOpenAI\u003c/code\u003e client).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"from swarm import Swarm\n\nclient = Swarm()\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efrom\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eswarm\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003eSwarm\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eclient\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003eSwarm\u003c/span\u003e()\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eclient.run()\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-clientrun\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: client.run()\" href=\"#clientrun\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSwarm's \u003ccode\u003erun()\u003c/code\u003e function is analogous to the \u003ccode\u003echat.completions.create()\u003c/code\u003e function in the Chat Completions API  it takes \u003ccode\u003emessages\u003c/code\u003e and returns \u003ccode\u003emessages\u003c/code\u003e and saves no state between calls. Importantly, however, it also handles Agent function execution, hand-offs, context variable references, and can take multiple turns before returning to the user.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAt its core, Swarm's \u003ccode\u003eclient.run()\u003c/code\u003e implements the following loop:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eGet a completion from the current Agent\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eExecute tool calls and append results\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSwitch Agent if necessary\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUpdate context variables, if necessary\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIf no new function calls, return\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch4 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eArguments\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-arguments\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Arguments\" href=\"#arguments\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 Only the \u003ccode\u003einstructions\u003c/code\u003e of the active \u003ccode\u003eAgent\u003c/code\u003e will be present at any given time (e.g. if there is an \u003ccode\u003eAgent\u003c/code\u003e handoff, the \u003ccode\u003esystem\u003c/code\u003e prompt will change, but the chat history will not.)\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"agent = Agent(\n   instructions=\u0026quot;You are a helpful agent.\u0026quot;\n)\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eagent\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003eAgent\u003c/span\u003e(\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003einstructions\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"You are a helpful agent.\"\u003c/span\u003e\n)\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe \u003ccode\u003einstructions\u003c/code\u003e can either be a regular \u003ccode\u003estr\u003c/code\u003e, or a function that returns a \u003ccode\u003estr\u003c/code\u003e. dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDocstrings are turned into the function \u003ccode\u003edescription\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eParameters without default values are set to \u003ccode\u003erequired\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eType hints are mapped to the parameter's \u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e (and default to \u003ccode\u003estring\u003c/code\u003e).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePer-parameter descriptions are not explicitly supported, but should work similarly if just added in the docstring. class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 fGqKFv"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eoaCFS js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/openai/swarm/blob/main/assets/logo.png"><img src="/openai/swarm/raw/main/assets/logo.png" alt="Swarm Logo" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Swarm (experimental, educational)</h1><a id="user-content-swarm-experimental-educational" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Swarm (experimental, educational)" href="#swarm-experimental-educational"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">An educational framework exploring ergonomic, lightweight multi-agent orchestration.</p>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p dir="auto">Swarm is currently an experimental sample framework intended to explore ergonomic interfaces for multi-agent systems. It is not intended to be used in production, and therefore has no official support. (This also means we will not be reviewing PRs or issues!)</p>
<p dir="auto">The primary goal of Swarm is to showcase the handoff &amp; routines patterns explored in the <a href="https://cookbook.openai.com/examples/orchestrating_agents" rel="nofollow">Orchestrating Agents: Handoffs &amp; Routines</a> cookbook. It is not meant as a standalone library, and is primarily for educational purposes.</p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Install</h2><a id="user-content-install" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Install" href="#install"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Requires Python 3.10+</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pip install git+ssh://git@github.com/openai/swarm.git"><pre>pip install git+ssh://git@github.com/openai/swarm.git</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">or</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pip install git+https://github.com/openai/swarm.git"><pre>pip install git+https://github.com/openai/swarm.git</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Usage</h2><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Usage" href="#usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from swarm import Swarm, Agent

client = Swarm()

def transfer_to_agent_b():
    return agent_b


agent_a = Agent(
    name=&quot;Agent A&quot;,
    instructions=&quot;You are a helpful agent.&quot;,
    functions=[transfer_to_agent_b],
)

agent_b = Agent(
    name=&quot;Agent B&quot;,
    instructions=&quot;Only speak in Haikus.&quot;,
)

response = client.run(
    agent=agent_a,
    messages=[{&quot;role&quot;: &quot;user&quot;, &quot;content&quot;: &quot;I want to talk to agent B.&quot;}],
)

print(response.messages[-1][&quot;content&quot;])"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">swarm</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Swarm</span>, <span class="pl-v">Agent</span>

<span class="pl-s1">client</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Swarm</span>()

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">transfer_to_agent_b</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">agent_b</span>


<span class="pl-s1">agent_a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Agent</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Agent A"</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">instructions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"You are a helpful agent."</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">functions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s1">transfer_to_agent_b</span>],
)

<span class="pl-s1">agent_b</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Agent</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Agent B"</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">instructions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Only speak in Haikus."</span>,
)

<span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">client</span>.<span class="pl-en">run</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">agent</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">agent_a</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">messages</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[{<span class="pl-s">"role"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"user"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"content"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"I want to talk to agent B."</span>}],
)

<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-s1">messages</span>[<span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>][<span class="pl-s">"content"</span>])</pre></div>

New paths converge gracefully,
What can I assist?"><pre class="notranslate"><code>Hope glimmers brightly,

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Overview</h1><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Overview" href="#overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Swarm focuses on making agent <strong>coordination</strong> and <strong>execution</strong> lightweight, highly controllable, and easily testable.</p>
<p dir="auto">It accomplishes this through two primitive abstractions: <code>Agent</code>s and <strong>handoffs</strong>. An <code>Agent</code> encompasses <code>instructions</code> and <code>tools</code>, and can at any point choose to hand off a conversation to another <code>Agent</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">These primitives are powerful enough to express rich dynamics between tools and networks of agents, allowing you to build scalable, real-world solutions while avoiding a steep learning curve.</p>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p><p dir="auto">Swarm Agents are not related to Assistants in the Assistants API. They are named similarly for convenience, but are otherwise completely unrelated. Swarm is entirely powered by the Chat Completions API and is hence stateless between calls.</p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why Swarm</h2><a id="user-content-why-swarm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why Swarm" href="#why-swarm"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Swarm explores patterns that are lightweight, scalable, and highly customizable by design. Approaches similar to Swarm are best suited for situations dealing with a large number of independent capabilities and instructions that are difficult to encode into a single prompt.</p>
<p dir="auto">The Assistants API is a great option for developers looking for fully-hosted threads and built in memory management and retrieval. However, Swarm is an educational resource for developers curious to learn about multi-agent orchestration. Swarm runs (almost) entirely on the client and, much like the Chat Completions API, does not store state between calls.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Examples</h1><a id="user-content-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Examples" href="#examples"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Check out <code>/examples</code> for inspiration! Learn more about each one in its README.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="/openai/swarm/blob/main/examples/basic"><code>basic</code></a>: Simple examples of fundamentals like setup, function calling, handoffs, and context variables</li>
<li><a href="/openai/swarm/blob/main/examples/triage_agent"><code>triage_agent</code></a>: Simple example of setting up a basic triage step to hand off to the right agent</li>
<li><a href="/openai/swarm/blob/main/examples/weather_agent"><code>weather_agent</code></a>: Simple example of function calling</li>
<li><a href="/openai/swarm/blob/main/examples/airline"><code>airline</code></a>: A multi-agent setup for handling different customer service requests in an airline context.</li>
<li><a href="/openai/swarm/blob/main/examples/support_bot"><code>support_bot</code></a>: A customer service bot which includes a user interface agent and a help center agent with several tools</li>
<li><a href="/openai/swarm/blob/main/examples/personal_shopper"><code>personal_shopper</code></a>: A personal shopping agent that can help with making sales and refunding orders</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Documentation</h1><a id="user-content-documentation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Documentation" href="#documentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/openai/swarm/blob/main/assets/swarm_diagram.png"><img src="/openai/swarm/raw/main/assets/swarm_diagram.png" alt="Swarm Diagram" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Running Swarm</h2><a id="user-content-running-swarm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Running Swarm" href="#running-swarm"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Start by instantiating a Swarm client (which internally just instantiates an <code>OpenAI</code> client).</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from swarm import Swarm

client = Swarm()"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">swarm</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Swarm</span>

<span class="pl-s1">client</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Swarm</span>()</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>client.run()</code></h3><a id="user-content-clientrun" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: client.run()" href="#clientrun"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Swarm's <code>run()</code> function is analogous to the <code>chat.completions.create()</code> function in the Chat Completions API  it takes <code>messages</code> and returns <code>messages</code> and saves no state between calls. Importantly, however, it also handles Agent function execution, hand-offs, context variable references, and can take multiple turns before returning to the user.</p>
<p dir="auto">At its core, Swarm's <code>client.run()</code> implements the following loop:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Get a completion from the current Agent</li>
<li>Execute tool calls and append results</li>
<li>Switch Agent if necessary</li>
<li>Update context variables, if necessary</li>
<li>If no new function calls, return</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Arguments</h4><a id="user-content-arguments" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Arguments" href="#arguments"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<td><strong>agent</strong></td>
<td><code>Agent</code></td>
<td>The (initial) agent to be called.</td>
<td>(required)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>messages</strong></td>
<td><code>List</code></td>
<td>A list of message objects, identical to <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/api-reference/chat/create#chat-create-messages" rel="nofollow">Chat Completions <code>messages</code></a></td>
<td>(required)</td>
</tr>

<td><code>dict</code></td>

</tr>

<td><code>int</code></td>

<td><code>str</code></td>
<td>An optional string to override the model being used by an Agent</td>

<td><code>bool</code></td>
<td>If <code>False</code>, interrupt execution and immediately returns <code>tool_calls</code> message when an Agent tries to call a function</td>
<td><code>True</code></td>
</tr>

<td><code>bool</code></td>
<td>If <code>True</code>, enables streaming responses</td>
<td><code>False</code></td>
</tr>

<td><strong>debug</strong></td>
<td><code>bool</code></td>
<td>If <code>True</code>, enables debug logging</td>
<td><code>False</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto">Once <code>client.run()</code> is finished (after potentially multiple calls to agents and tools) it will return a <code>Response</code> containing all the relevant updated state. Specifically, the new <code>messages</code>, the last <code>Agent</code> to be called, and the most up-to-date <code>context_variables</code>. You can pass these values (plus new user messages) in to your next execution of <code>client.run()</code> to continue the interaction where it left off  much like <code>chat.completions.create()</code>. (The <code>run_demo_loop</code> function implements an example of a full execution loop in <code>/swarm/repl/repl.py</code>.)</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>Response</code> Fields</h4><a id="user-content-response-fields" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Response Fields" href="#response-fields"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

</tr>

<td><code>List</code></td>
<td>A list of message objects generated during the conversation. Very similar to <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/api-reference/chat/create#chat-create-messages" rel="nofollow">Chat Completions <code>messages</code></a>, but with a <code>sender</code> field indicating which <code>Agent</code> the message originated from.</td>

<td>The same as the input variables, plus any changes.</td>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Agents</h2><a id="user-content-agents" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Agents" href="#agents"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">An <code>Agent</code> simply encapsulates a set of <code>instructions</code> with a set of <code>functions</code> (plus some additional settings below), and has the capability to hand off execution to another <code>Agent</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">While it's tempting to personify an <code>Agent</code> as "someone who does X", it can also be used to represent a very specific workflow or step defined by a set of <code>instructions</code> and <code>functions</code> (e.g. a set of steps, a complex retrieval, single step of data transformation, etc). This allows <code>Agent</code>s to be composed into a network of "agents", "workflows", and "tasks", all represented by the same primitive.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>Agent</code> Fields</h2><a id="user-content-agent-fields" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Agent Fields" href="#agent-fields"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Type</th>
<th>Description</th>
<th>Default</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>name</strong></td>
<td><code>str</code></td>
<td>The name of the agent.</td>
<td><code>"Agent"</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>model</strong></td>
<td><code>str</code></td>
<td>The model to be used by the agent.</td>
<td><code>"gpt-4o"</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>instructions</strong></td>
<td><code>str</code> or <code>func() -&gt; str</code></td>
<td>Instructions for the agent, can be a string or a callable returning a string.</td>
<td><code>"You are a helpful agent."</code></td>
</tr>

<td><code>List</code></td>

<td><code>[]</code></td>
</tr>

<td><code>str</code></td>
<td>The tool choice for the agent, if any.</td>
<td><code>None</code></td>

</tbody>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Instructions</h3><a id="user-content-instructions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Instructions" href="#instructions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>Agent</code> <code>instructions</code> are directly converted into the <code>system</code> prompt of a conversation (as the first message). Only the <code>instructions</code> of the active <code>Agent</code> will be present at any given time (e.g. if there is an <code>Agent</code> handoff, the <code>system</code> prompt will change, but the chat history will not.)</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="agent = Agent(
   instructions=&quot;You are a helpful agent.&quot;
)"><pre><span class="pl-s1">agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Agent</span>(
   <span class="pl-s1">instructions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"You are a helpful agent."</span>
)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>instructions</code> can either be a regular <code>str</code>, or a function that returns a <code>str</code>. The function can optionally receive a <code>context_variables</code> parameter, which will be populated by the <code>context_variables</code> passed into <code>client.run()</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def instructions(context_variables):
   user_name = context_variables[&quot;user_name&quot;]
   return f&quot;Help the user, {user_name}, do whatever they want.&quot;

agent = Agent(
   instructions=instructions
)
response = client.run(
   agent=agent,
   messages=[{&quot;role&quot;:&quot;user&quot;, &quot;content&quot;: &quot;Hi!&quot;}],
   context_variables={&quot;user_name&quot;:&quot;John&quot;}
)
print(response.messages[-1][&quot;content&quot;])"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">instructions</span>(<span class="pl-s1">context_variables</span>):
   <span class="pl-s1">user_name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">context_variables</span>[<span class="pl-s">"user_name"</span>]
   <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">f"Help the user, <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">user_name</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>, do whatever they want."</span>

<span class="pl-s1">agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Agent</span>(
   <span class="pl-s1">instructions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">instructions</span>
)
<span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">client</span>.<span class="pl-en">run</span>(
   <span class="pl-s1">agent</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">agent</span>,
   <span class="pl-s1">messages</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[{<span class="pl-s">"role"</span>:<span class="pl-s">"user"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"content"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Hi!"</span>}],
   <span class="pl-s1">context_variables</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>{<span class="pl-s">"user_name"</span>:<span class="pl-s">"John"</span>}
)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-s1">messages</span>[<span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>][<span class="pl-s">"content"</span>])</pre></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Hi John, how can I assist you today?"><pre class="notranslate"><code>Hi John, how can I assist you today?
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Functions</h2><a id="user-content-functions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Functions" href="#functions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Swarm <code>Agent</code>s can call python functions directly.</li>
<li>Function should usually return a <code>str</code> (values will be attempted to be cast as a <code>str</code>).</li>
<li>If a function returns an <code>Agent</code>, execution will be transferred to that <code>Agent</code>.</li>
<li>If a function defines a <code>context_variables</code> parameter, it will be populated by the <code>context_variables</code> passed into <code>client.run()</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def greet(context_variables, language):
   user_name = context_variables[&quot;user_name&quot;]
   greeting = &quot;Hola&quot; if language.lower() == &quot;spanish&quot; else &quot;Hello&quot;
   print(f&quot;{greeting}, {user_name}!&quot;)
   return &quot;Done&quot;

agent = Agent(
   functions=[greet]
)

client.run(
   agent=agent,
   messages=[{&quot;role&quot;: &quot;user&quot;, &quot;content&quot;: &quot;Usa greet() por favor.&quot;}],
   context_variables={&quot;user_name&quot;: &quot;John&quot;}
)"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">greet</span>(<span class="pl-s1">context_variables</span>, <span class="pl-s1">language</span>):
   <span class="pl-s1">user_name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">context_variables</span>[<span class="pl-s">"user_name"</span>]
   <span class="pl-s1">greeting</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">"Hola"</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">language</span>.<span class="pl-en">lower</span>() <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">"spanish"</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-s">"Hello"</span>
   <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">greeting</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>, <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">user_name</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>!"</span>)
   <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">"Done"</span>

<span class="pl-s1">agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Agent</span>(
   <span class="pl-s1">functions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s1">greet</span>]
)

<span class="pl-s1">client</span>.<span class="pl-en">run</span>(
   <span class="pl-s1">agent</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">agent</span>,
   <span class="pl-s1">messages</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[{<span class="pl-s">"role"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"user"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"content"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Usa greet() por favor."</span>}],
   <span class="pl-s1">context_variables</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>{<span class="pl-s">"user_name"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"John"</span>}
)</pre></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Hola, John!"><pre class="notranslate"><code>Hola, John!
</code></pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If an <code>Agent</code> function call has an error (missing function, wrong argument, error) an error response will be appended to the chat so the <code>Agent</code> can recover gracefully.</li>
<li>If multiple functions are called by the <code>Agent</code>, they will be executed in that order.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Handoffs and Updating Context Variables</h3><a id="user-content-handoffs-and-updating-context-variables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Handoffs and Updating Context Variables" href="#handoffs-and-updating-context-variables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">An <code>Agent</code> can hand off to another <code>Agent</code> by returning it in a <code>function</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sales_agent = Agent(name=&quot;Sales Agent&quot;)

def transfer_to_sales():
   return sales_agent

agent = Agent(functions=[transfer_to_sales])

response = client.run(agent, [{&quot;role&quot;:&quot;user&quot;, &quot;content&quot;:&quot;Transfer me to sales.&quot;}])
print(response.agent.name)"><pre><span class="pl-s1">sales_agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Agent</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Sales Agent"</span>)

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">transfer_to_sales</span>():
   <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">sales_agent</span>

<span class="pl-s1">agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Agent</span>(<span class="pl-s1">functions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s1">transfer_to_sales</span>])

<span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">client</span>.<span class="pl-en">run</span>(<span class="pl-s1">agent</span>, [{<span class="pl-s">"role"</span>:<span class="pl-s">"user"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"content"</span>:<span class="pl-s">"Transfer me to sales."</span>}])
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-s1">agent</span>.<span class="pl-s1">name</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Sales Agent"><pre class="notranslate"><code>Sales Agent
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">It can also update the <code>context_variables</code> by returning a more complete <code>Result</code> object. This can also contain a <code>value</code> and an <code>agent</code>, in case you want a single function to return a value, update the agent, and update the context variables (or any subset of the three).</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sales_agent = Agent(name=&quot;Sales Agent&quot;)

def talk_to_sales():
   print(&quot;Hello, World!&quot;)
   return Result(
       value=&quot;Done&quot;,
       agent=sales_agent,
       context_variables={&quot;department&quot;: &quot;sales&quot;}
   )

agent = Agent(functions=[talk_to_sales])

response = client.run(
   agent=agent,
   messages=[{&quot;role&quot;: &quot;user&quot;, &quot;content&quot;: &quot;Transfer me to sales&quot;}],
   context_variables={&quot;user_name&quot;: &quot;John&quot;}
)
print(response.agent.name)
print(response.context_variables)"><pre><span class="pl-s1">sales_agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Agent</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Sales Agent"</span>)

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">talk_to_sales</span>():
   <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Hello, World!"</span>)
   <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-v">Result</span>(
       <span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Done"</span>,
       <span class="pl-s1">agent</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">sales_agent</span>,
       <span class="pl-s1">context_variables</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>{<span class="pl-s">"department"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"sales"</span>}
   )

<span class="pl-s1">agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Agent</span>(<span class="pl-s1">functions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s1">talk_to_sales</span>])

<span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">client</span>.<span class="pl-en">run</span>(
   <span class="pl-s1">agent</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">agent</span>,
   <span class="pl-s1">messages</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[{<span class="pl-s">"role"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"user"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"content"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Transfer me to sales"</span>}],
   <span class="pl-s1">context_variables</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>{<span class="pl-s">"user_name"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"John"</span>}
)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-s1">agent</span>.<span class="pl-s1">name</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-s1">context_variables</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Sales Agent
{'department': 'sales', 'user_name': 'John'}"><pre class="notranslate"><code>Sales Agent
{'department': 'sales', 'user_name': 'John'}
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p><p dir="auto">If an <code>Agent</code> calls multiple functions to hand-off to an <code>Agent</code>, only the last handoff function will be used.</p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function Schemas</h3><a id="user-content-function-schemas" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function Schemas" href="#function-schemas"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Swarm automatically converts functions into a JSON Schema that is passed into Chat Completions <code>tools</code>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Docstrings are turned into the function <code>description</code>.</li>
<li>Parameters without default values are set to <code>required</code>.</li>
<li>Type hints are mapped to the parameter's <code>type</code> (and default to <code>string</code>).</li>
<li>Per-parameter descriptions are not explicitly supported, but should work similarly if just added in the docstring. (In the future docstring argument parsing may be added.)</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def greet(name, age: int, location: str = &quot;New York&quot;):
   &quot;&quot;&quot;Greets the user. Make sure to get their name and age before calling.

   Args:
      name: Name of the user.
      age: Age of the user.
      location: Best place on earth.
   &quot;&quot;&quot;
   print(f&quot;Hello {name}, glad you are {age} in {location}!&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">greet</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span>, <span class="pl-s1">age</span>: <span class="pl-s1">int</span>, <span class="pl-s1">location</span>: <span class="pl-s1">str</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">"New York"</span>):
   <span class="pl-s">"""Greets the user. Make sure to get their name and age before calling.</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">   Args:</span>
<span class="pl-s">      name: Name of the user.</span>
<span class="pl-s">      age: Age of the user.</span>
<span class="pl-s">      location: Best place on earth.</span>
<span class="pl-s">   """</span>
   <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"Hello <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>, glad you are <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">age</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> in <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">location</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>!"</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
   &quot;type&quot;: &quot;function&quot;,
   &quot;function&quot;: {
      &quot;name&quot;: &quot;greet&quot;,
      &quot;description&quot;: &quot;Greets the user. Make sure to get their name and age before calling.\n\nArgs:\n   name: Name of the user.\n   age: Age of the user.\n   location: Best place on earth.&quot;,
      &quot;parameters&quot;: {
         &quot;type&quot;: &quot;object&quot;,
         &quot;properties&quot;: {
            &quot;name&quot;: {&quot;type&quot;: &quot;string&quot;},
            &quot;age&quot;: {&quot;type&quot;: &quot;integer&quot;},
            &quot;location&quot;: {&quot;type&quot;: &quot;string&quot;}
         },
         &quot;required&quot;: [&quot;name&quot;, &quot;age&quot;]
      }
   }
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"function"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
   <span class="pl-s">"function"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"greet"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Greets the user. Make sure to get their name and age before calling.\n\nArgs:\n   name: Name of the user.\n   age: Age of the user.\n   location: Best place on earth."</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"parameters"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
         <span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"object"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
         <span class="pl-s">"properties"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"string"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-s">"age"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"integer"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-s">"location"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"string"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
         <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
         <span class="pl-s">"required"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"name"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"age"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
   <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Streaming</h2><a id="user-content-streaming" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Streaming" href="#streaming"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="stream = client.run(agent, messages, stream=True)
for chunk in stream:
   print(chunk)"><pre><span class="pl-s1">stream</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">client</span>.<span class="pl-en">run</span>(<span class="pl-s1">agent</span>, <span class="pl-s1">messages</span>, <span class="pl-s1">stream</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>)
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">chunk</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">stream</span>:
   <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">chunk</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Uses the same events as <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/api-reference/streaming" rel="nofollow">Chat Completions API streaming</a>. See <code>process_and_print_streaming_response</code> in <code>/swarm/repl/repl.py</code> as an example.</p>
<p dir="auto">Two new event types have been added:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>{"delim":"start"}</code> and <code>{"delim":"end"}</code>, to signal each time an <code>Agent</code> handles a single message (response or function call). This helps identify switches between <code>Agent</code>s.</li>
<li><code>{"response": Response}</code> will return a <code>Response</code> object at the end of a stream with the aggregated (complete) response, for convenience.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Evaluations</h1><a id="user-content-evaluations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Evaluations" href="#evaluations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Evaluations are crucial to any project, and we encourage developers to bring their own eval suites to test the performance of their swarms. For reference, we have some examples for how to eval swarm in the <code>airline</code>, <code>weather_agent</code> and <code>triage_agent</code> quickstart examples. See the READMEs for more details.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Utils</h1><a id="user-content-utils" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Utils" href="#utils"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Use the <code>run_demo_loop</code> to test out your swarm! This will run a REPL on your command line. Supports streaming.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from swarm.repl import run_demo_loop
...
run_demo_loop(agent, stream=True)"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">swarm</span>.<span class="pl-s1">repl</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">run_demo_loop</span>
...
<span class="pl-en">run_demo_loop</span>(<span class="pl-s1">agent</span>, <span class="pl-s1">stream</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Core Contributors</h1><a id="user-content-core-contributors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Core Contributors" href="#core-contributors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
